    5. One of the two rooms we booked had an obvious sewer smell when we first entered the room.
    The hotel price is not cheap among hotels in Leshan, but overall the experience is very poor. The hotel itself advertises itself as a luxury hotel, but the actual services provided are almost non-existent, even inferior to some ordinary small hotels. This time I am completely disappointed with the Amber brand and will never stay here again.
